### Round 3: Chinese Grand Prix
*Date: 2011-04-17*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 18: Abu Dhabi Grand Prix
*Date: 2011-11-13*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
